 Thank you so much for all your wishes üôè I'm still in the hospital recovering, and will be sharing my birth story soon :) # babyboy xxrep 24 _ # chhavimittal # pregnancy # boy # son # motherhood # motherandsona post shared bychhavi Mittal (@chhavihussein ) onmay 13, 2019 at 9:02 pm pdtview this post on instagramthe 10th MONTH
 
 
 Here i am, thinking i have seen it all and heard it all
 
 
 But in the 11th hour of my pregnancy, there's yet another myth that i need to address! The 10th month
 Yes, there is a 10th month in pregnancy, and I'm currently living it
 So many people tried to correct me in one of my recent posts, thinking i may have accidentally written 10th instead of 9th
 No it was no accident
 The 10th month, as logic suggests, starts after the 9th month ends
 After 36 weeks of pregnancy, the baby is officially ready to come into this world
 40 weeks is considered a full term, and that's when the doctor gives you your EDD (estimated due date)
 The due date is always ESTIMATED because nobody can predict when the baby arrives
 It is extremely common and absolutely normal for women to reach 42 weeks before natural labor begins
 
 especially if it's the second pregnancy
 
 
 and once you cross 38 / 39 weeks, your 10th month begins
 So, while my clock ticks, i could go into labor right this minute, or another week later
 
 
 I'm not worried
 On the contrary, I'm rather relaxed
 Because i know, once the baby comes, I'll have my hands full! And i think now is the perfect time to also say that it's always the baby who decides when labour will begin
 So you can try all you want, get restless, get scans done, pray that the baby comes out fast (I know it's uncomfortable)
 
 
 But trust me, the baby is the most comfortable inside you! So don't hold your breath
 
 
 But remember, good things come to those who wait

 The Nirbhaya Fund was started by the Central Government after the Nirbhaya rape scandal that rocked the country
 iskaa makasad desh bhar main balaatkaar peeditaaon kaa punarvaas or unhen aarthik madad muhaiyaa karana tha
 The funds of this fund, which started in 2014, have either not been used for many years or a very small amount has been distributed
 aisa nahin he ki fund banane ke baad se deshbhar main balaatkaar hone hi band ho gaye

 ab is maamle main madhya pradesh sarkaar kii berukhi bhi saamne ai he
 Madhya Pradesh has got most part of the Nirbhaya Fund, but the government gives only six and a half thousand rupees to the rape victims
 supreme court main pesh halafname ke jariye shivaraj sarkaar ne bataaya ki pichley saal rajya bhar main rape ke 1951 maamle darj hue
 All the victims were given compensation of six thousand to six and a half thousand rupees
 is par justise madan bi lokur or justise deepak gupta kii peeth ne naaraaz hote hue poocha ki ye aap kya kar rahe hai? or aap aisa kaise kar sakate hai? ye kya daan kii raashi he?darasal supreme court main balaatkaar peeditaaon kii doctorl jaanch ke taur tareekon par uthaai gai aapattiyon kii yachika par sunwaayee chal rahi thi
 The court asked that the last time all state governments were asked for answers, what have they done for the rehabilitation and help of rape victims? The Madhya Pradesh government filed its affidavit on this
 ise padhate hi court ne fouran fatkaar lagaai or madhya pradesh sarkaar ko khari-khari sunai
 Angry court said to Madhya Pradesh government that are you donating this? Rape worth 6000 rupees? How can you do this? The Madhya Pradesh government said in the court that it has given compensation of Rs 6000 to 6500 to each victim in 1951 cases of rape registered last year
